model.param.set('w2', '54*w11');

model.component('comp1').func.create('an3', 'Analytic');
model.component('comp1').func.create('an4', 'Analytic');

model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('I_el', 'if( w1n <= 0, 0,quad( (zn - a1)^(1.5) * exp(-0.5*(alpha1*zn)^2),zn, a1, a1 + w1n ) )');
model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('I_ep', 'if( w2n <= w1n, 0,quad( (zn - a1) * exp(-0.5*(alpha1*zn)^2)* ( 1 - 0.6*( log(w2) - log( sigma*(zn - a1) ) )/( log(w2) - log(w11) ) ) * ( 1 - 2*(( sigma*(zn - a1) - w11 )/( w2 - w11 ))^3+ 3*(( sigma*(zn - a1) - w11 )/( w2 - w11 ))^2 ),zn, a1 + w11n, a1 + w2n ) )');
model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('m1', 'alpha1*(a1 + w2n)');
model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('Qm', '0.5*erfc( m1/sqrt(2) )');
model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('J_pl', '(1/(alpha1)^2)*exp(-0.5*m1^2) - (a1/alpha1)*(sqrt(2*pi)*Qm)');
model.component('comp1').variable('var7').set('pr', '(2/3)*E0*nasp*sqrt(beta)*sigma^(1.5) * (sigma/ss)*(1/sqrt(2*pi)) * I_el + (pi)*hd*nasp*beta*sigma   * (sigma/ss)*(1/sqrt(2*pi)) * I_ep + (2*pi)*hd*nasp*beta*sigma  * (sigma/ss)*(1/sqrt(2*pi)) * J_pl');
